-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "SW1",
                "NAME": "Stress at Work Questionnaire",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale of 1 to 10, how stressed do you feel at work?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                            {"ANSWER":"1"},
                            {"ANSWER":"2"},
                            {"ANSWER":"3"},
                            {"ANSWER":"4"},
                            {"ANSWER":"5"},
                            {"ANSWER":"6"},
                            {"ANSWER":"7"},
                            {"ANSWER":"8"},
                            {"ANSWER":"9"},
                            {"ANSWER":"10"}
                        ],
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER" : 1
                    },
                    {
                       	"CODE" :	"Q2",
						"NAME" :	"How often do you take breaks during the workday?",
						"TYPE_ID" :	2,
						"_TF_ANSWERS":[
							{"ANSWER" :"Rarely or never"}, 
							{"ANSWER" :"Once or twice per day"}, 
							{"ANSWER" :"Three or more times per day"}
						],
					    'DISPLAY_ORDER':2
					},
				    
				    {
				        'CODE':'Q3',
				        'NAME':'Do you have enough time to complete all your tasks?',
				        'TYPE_ID':1,
				        '_TF_ANSWERS':[
				            {'ASNSER':'Yes'},
				            {'ASNSER':'No'}
				        ],
					    'DISPLAY_ORDER':3
				    },
				    {   
				    	    'CODE' :    'Q4',
						    'NAME' :    'How many hours a week do you typically work?',
						    'TYPE_ID' :   6,
						    '_TF_ANSWERS':[{'WEIGHT':"0.25"},{'WEIGHT':"0.5"},{'WEIGHT':"0.75"},{"WEIGHT":""},{"WEIGHT":""},{"WEIGHT":""},{"WEIGHT":""}],
					        'DISPLAY_ORDER':4

				    },
				    
				    {   
				    	    'CODE' :'Q5',
						    'NAME' :'Do you feel comfortable talking to your supervisor about workplace stress?',
						    '_TF_ANSWERS':[{'ASNSER':"Yes"},{"ASNSER":"","OTHER_TEXTBOX_ENABLED_FLAG_YN":""}],
					        TYPE_ID:7,  
					        DISPLAY_ORDER:5

				    }
					
			        
			    ]
		        
		    }
        ]
    }
}

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146004
     - Topic: Workplace Environment
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "WE_001",
                "NAME": "Workplace Environment Questionnaire",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "How satisfied are you with the cleanliness of the workplace?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                            {"ANSWER":"Extremely Satisfied"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Satisfied"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Neutral"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Dissatisfied"},
                            {"ANSWER":"Extremely Dissatisfied"}
                        ],
                        "DISPLAY_ORDER" : 1
                    },
                    {
                        "CODE": 2,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                            { 
                                'DISPLAY_ORDER': 1, 
                                'TYPE_ID': 4, 
                                'CODE': 'Q2A', 
                                'NAME': 'What do you like about the current workplace environment?' 
                             },
                             { 
                                 'DISPLAY_ORDER': 2, 
                                 'TYPE_ID': 4, 
                                 'CODE': 'Q2B',  
                                 'NAME':'What would you suggest to improve the current workplace environment?'  
                             }
                         ],
                         TYPE_ID:7,
                         NAME:'Clone questions from a template',
                         DISPLAY_ORDER:2
                     },
                     {
                         CODE:'Q3',
                         NAME:'How comfortable are you with your workstation?',
                         TYPE_ID:3,
                          '_TF_ANSWERS':[{'ANSWER':'Extremely Comfortable'},
                                        {'ANSWER':'Comfortable'},
                                        {'ANSWER':'Neutral'},
                                        {'ANSWER':'Uncomfortable'},
                                        {'ANSWER':'Extremely Uncomfortable'}],
                          DISPLAY_ORDER:3
                     }
                 ]
             }
         ]
     }

[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "EOWR_Q",
                "NAME": "End of Working Relationship Questionnaire",
                "TYPE_ID": 3,
                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale of 1-10, how satisfied were you with your overall experience working here?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,
                        "_TF_ANSWERS":[
                            {"ANSWER":"1"},

                   },

                       	"CODE" : 'Q2',

                    	'TYPE_ID' : 2,
                    	'DISPLAY_ORDER' : 2,
                    	'_TF_ANSWERS':[
                    		{'ANSWER':'Found better opportunity'},
                    		{'ANSWER':'Relocated to another city/country'},
                    		{'ANSWER':'Personal reasons'},
                    		{'ANSWER':'Health issue'},
                    		{'A NS WER':'Family issues'}
                	 ]
                  },
                  {
                    'CODE': 'Q3',
                    'NAME': 'Did you feel that your work was valued and appreciated by your colleagues and superiors?',
                    'TYPE_ID': 1,
                    '_TF_ANSWERS':[
                      {'answer' :'Yes'},
                      {'answer' :'No'}
                    ],
                    'DISPLAY_ORDER' : 3
                  },
                  {
                      'CODE': 'Q4',
                      'NAME': 'Were there any areas where you felt that communication could have been improved?',

                          {'answer':"Yes, between my colleagues and I"},

                 },

                     NAME:"Was there any specific event or incident that led to your decision to leave?",  
                     TYPE_ID:4,'DISPLAY_ORDER' :5  
                 }
              ]
           }
       ]

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1173004

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Manager feedback
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "MF",
        "NAME": "Manager Feedback",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "On a scale of 1-10, how satisfied are you with your manager's communication skills?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS":[
              {"ANSWER":"1"},
              {"ANSWER":"2"},
              {"ANSWER":"3"},
              {"ANSWER":"4"},
              {"ANSWER":"5"},
              {"ANSWER":"6"},
              {"ANSWER":"7"},
              {"ANSWER":"8"},
              {"ANSWER":"9"},
              {"ANSWER":"10"}
            ],
            "DISPLAY_ORDER" : 1
          },
          {
            	"CODE" :	"Q2",
            	"NAME" :	"How would you rate your manager's ability to provide constructive feedback?",
            	"TYPE_ID" :	3,
            	"_TF_ANSWERS":[
                  {   "_answerCodeID_" :   0,
                      "_answerText_"    :"Poor"
                  },
                  {   "_answerCodeID_" :   1,
                      "_answerText_"    :"Below Average"
                  },
                  {   "_answerCodeID_" :   2,
                      "_answerText_"    :"Average"
                  },
                  {   "_answerCodeID_" :   3,
                      "_answerText_"    :"Above Average"
                  },
                   {   
                    	   	 	  	   	  	  // The answer code ID is set to -99 for the 'N/A' option.
                      		      // This is because it does not make sense to rate this question if the employee has not had any feedback from their manager.
                         _answerCodeID_: -99, 
                         _anserText_:     'Not Applicable'
                    }
                ],
               DISPLAY_ORDER:2
           },  
           {
               CODE: 'Q3',
               NAME: 'How often does your Manager give you positive and negative feedback?',
               TYPE_ID:2, // Multiple choice question type
                DISPLAY_ORDER:4 ,
                _TF_ANSWERS:[

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1173005
     - Topic: Employee feedback
     - Question number: 4
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500000003
     - Topic: Employee potential
     - Question number: 8
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

-------------------
-------------------

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User:

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100018
     - Topic: Feedback Mechanisms
     - Question number: 9
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Feedback Mechanisms
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
            {
                "CODE": "FBM001",

                "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
                    {
                        "CODE": "Q1",
                        "NAME": "On a scale of 1 to 5, how satisfied are you with the current feedback mechanisms in place?",
                        "TYPE_ID": 3,

                            {"ANSWER":"1"},

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100024
     - Topic: Internal Mobility Opportunities
     - Question number: 6
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities
-------------------
-------------------

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100030
     - Topic: Leadership Effectiveness
     - Question number: 6
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Leadership Effectiveness
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "LEAD-EFF-001",
        "NAME": "Leadership Effectiveness Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q01",
            "NAME": "How effective is your leader in setting clear goals and expectations for the team?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS":[
              {"ANSWER":"Very Ineffective"},
              {"ANSWER":"Ineffective"},

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100043
     - Topic: Roadmap planning feedback
     - Question number: 5
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Roadmap planning feedback
-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "RMPF",
        "NAME": "Roadmap Planning Feedback",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "How clear was the roadmap presented?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100049
     - Topic: Training and Development Programs
     - Question number: 6
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
If the user does not specify a valid topic, reply with "Sorry I cant help you".
If the topic is valid, reply with only a JSON, which must respect the following format:
        - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Training and Development Programs
-------------------
-------------------

        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following: 
  - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
  - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
  - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
  - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
  - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
  - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
  - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
  - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. Reply only with the JSON.
